</script><div id="calendar" class="theme-border">
<script type="text/javascript">
(function(){
    var calendar = {
        init: function (opt) {
            this.solarCalendarDate = opt.solarCalendarDate;
            this.weekDate = opt.weekDate;
            this.lunarCalendarDate = opt.lunarCalendarDate;
            this.whiteList = opt.whiteList;
            this.solarTopicText = this.getTopicText(this.solarCalendarDate);
            this.lunarTopicText = this.getTopicText(this.lunarCalendarDate);
            this.topicText = this.lunarTopicText || this.solarTopicText;
            this.topicTextUrl = this.getUrl(this.topicText);
            this.render();
        },
        render: function () {
            var html = this.getHtml();
            hao360.docWrite(html);
        },
        getHtml: function () {
            var htmlTpl = [
                '<a href="http://hao.360.com/rili">',
                    this.solarCalendarDate + this.weekDate,
                '</a>',
                '<div>',
                    '<a href="' + this.topicTextUrl + '">',
                        this.topicText && this.topicText[0] || this.lunarCalendarDate,
                    '</a>',
                '</div>'
            ];
            return htmlTpl.join('');
        },
        getTopicText: function (date) {
            return this.whiteList[date];
        },
        getUrl: function (text) {
            var url = 'http://hao.360.com/rili';
            url = text && text[1] ? text[1] : url;
            return url;
        }
    }

    var e = hao360.todayObj,
        solarCalendarDate = [e.getMonth() + 1, "\u6708", e.getDate(), "\u65e5"].join(""),
        weekDate = ["\u5468\u65e5", "\u5468\u4e00", "\u5468\u4e8c", "\u5468\u4e09", "\u5468\u56db", "\u5468\u4e94", "\u5468\u516d"][e.getDay()],
        lunarCalendarDate = hao360.lunar(e);

    var whiteList = {
        '正月初一': ['春节'],
        '正月十五': ['元宵节'],
        '五月初五': ['端午节'],
        '七月初七': ['七夕'],
        '九月初九': ['重阳节'],
        '腊月初八': ['腊八节'],
        '1月1日': ['元旦'],
        '3月8日': ['三八妇女节'],
        '5月1日': ['五一劳动节'],
        '6月1日': ['六一儿童节'],
        '9月10日': ['教师节'],
        '10月1日': ['国庆节']
    };
    calendar.init({
        solarCalendarDate: solarCalendarDate,
        weekDate: weekDate,
        lunarCalendarDate: lunarCalendarDate,
        whiteList: qboot.mix(specialFestivalConf || {}, whiteList)
    });
})();
</script>

                (function(){
                    var config = HAO_CONFIG.search,
                        searchData = new AppData('api.hao.360.cn', config.r),
                        defaultEng = searchData.get('defaultEng')||"somulti",
                        g = hao360.g;
                    if(/^\?1009(\W|$)/.test(location.search)){
                        defaultEng = 'so360';
                        hao360.g('search-engine').className = 'single';
                    }

                    (function () {
                        var COOKIE_KEY = 'somultiswitch';
                        var cookieVal = qboot.cookie.get(COOKIE_KEY);

                        if (cookieVal === '1') {
                            LogHub.behavior('somultiswitch', 'soeng' + cookieVal);
                            return;
                        }

                        if (defaultEng === 'somulti') {
                            cookieValue = 1;
                            defaultEng = 'so360';
                            searchData.set('defaultEng', 'so360');
                            LogHub.behavior('somultiswitch', 'so360');

                            qboot.cookie.set(COOKIE_KEY, cookieValue, {expires: 30 * 24 * 3600 * 1000}); // 1 month
                        }
                    }());

                    if(defaultEng != 'somulti'){
                        var defaultEngData = HAO_DATA.searchTabData.searchEngConf.webpage[defaultEng];
                        if(defaultEngData){
                            g('eng-logo').className = defaultEng;
                            g('search-btn').innerHTML = defaultEngData[5] || defaultEngData[2] + '搜索';
                            g('search-kw').setAttribute('name', defaultEngData[1]);
                            g('search-form').setAttribute('action', defaultEngData[0]);

                            var defaultParamsEl = g('search-form').getElementsByTagName('div')[0],
                                paramsEl = document.createElement('div'),
                                paramsData = defaultEngData[4].split(';'),
                                paramsHtml = '';
                            paramsEl.className = 'others-params webpage-' + defaultEng + ' types-webpage';
                            while(paramsData.length){
                                var p = paramsData[0].split(':');
                                paramsHtml += '<input type="hidden" name="' + p[0] + '" value="' + p[1] + '">';
                                paramsData.shift();
                            }
                            paramsEl.innerHTML = paramsHtml;
                            g('search-form').insertBefore(paramsEl, defaultParamsEl);
                            g('search-form').removeChild(defaultParamsEl);
                        }
                    }else{
                        g('search-hsid').setAttribute('value', qboot.cookie.get('__hsid'));
                    }

                    // 宽屏版下搜索框加宽试验
                    g('search').className = 'searchbig';
                    

                })();
            </script>

<script>
    // 首页首屏最快速度渲染360热搜词  用soHotwords-fRecData缓存数据，之后接口数据来了，再替换
    ;(function(){
        var encode4Html = function(s) {
			var el = document.createElement('pre'); //这里要用pre，用div有时会丢失换行，例如：'a\r\n\r\nb'
			var text = document.createTextNode(s);
			el.appendChild(text);
			return el.innerHTML;
        };
        
        var fWrapTpl = '<ul>{content}</ul><a href="javascript:void(0);" data-state="expand" class="change"></a>',
            itemTpl = '<li data-from="{from}" data-m="{md5}" data-t="{type}" data-href="{url}" data-queryattr="{query_attr}" class="{className}" data-clk="{clk}" data-asin="{asin}"> \
                <a class="item" href="{url}" target="_blank" title="{title}" data-src="{src}">{icon}<span>{kw}</span>{ellipsis}{attr}</a> \
                <a href="javascript:void(0);" class="del" title="删除"></a> \
            </li>';

        // soHotwords-fRecData 首屏缓存数据
        var soHotwordsStorage = new AppData('api.hao.360.cn').get('soHotwords-fRecData'),
            content = [];
        
        if (soHotwordsStorage && soHotwordsStorage.length) {
            var length = soHotwordsStorage.length,
                item = null;

            for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
                item = soHotwordsStorage[i];
                item['icon'] = hao360.isHttps() ? hao360.convertHttpToHttps(item['icon']) : item['icon'];
                item.kw = encode4Html(item.kw);
                item.md5 = encode4Html(item.md5);
                item.title = encode4Html(item.title);
                content.push(R.tmpl(itemTpl, item));
            }

            var tmplData = {
                "content": content.join('')
            };
            
            R('so-hotword').render(fWrapTpl, tmplData);
        }

    }());
</script>

<script>
    (function () {
        var g = hao360.g;
        function TopActive (options) {
            this.$options = options;
            this.cookieName = 'top-activity-close'
            this.init();
        }
        var proto = TopActive.prototype;

        proto.init = function () {
            // 急速浏览器开关控制
            var isOn360ee = hao360.is360ee() && this.$options.isOn_360ee == 0;
            if (isOn360ee || this.verifyClose()) return;

            var startTime = this.$options.startTime;
            var endTime = this.$options.endTime;
            var date = hao360.queryUrl(location.href, 'previewTime');
            date = date ? new Date(date) : hao360.todayObj;
            if (date > startTime && date < endTime) {
                this.renderHTML();
                this.listenClose();
            }
        };

        proto.renderHTML = function () {
            var topActivity = g('top_activity');
            topActivity.innerHTML = g('lazyload_top_activity').value;
            topActivity.style.display = 'block';
        };

        proto.listenClose = function () {
            var self = this;
            g('top-activity__btn--close').onclick = function (ev) {
                self.close();
                ev.preventDefault();
            };
        };

        proto.close = function () {
            var cookieName = this.cookieName;
            var topActivity = g('top_activity');
            var oneDay = 1000 * 3600 * 24;
            g('doc-main-hd').removeChild(topActivity);
            LogHub.behavior('top_activity', 'close');
            qboot.cookie.set(cookieName, 1, {expires: oneDay});
        }

        proto.verifyClose = function () {
            var cookieName = this.cookieName;
            return qboot.cookie.get(cookieName);
        };

        new TopActive({
            startTime: new Date('2019/08/01 00:00:00'), // 上线时间
            endTime: new Date('2019/08/01 23:59:59'), //  下线时间
            isOn_360ee: 1 //极速浏览器 0关 1开
        });
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (function () {
        function TopHotsite () {
            this.init();
        }
        var proto = TopHotsite.prototype;

        proto.init = function () {
            this.cookieName = 'top-hotsite-close';
            this.id = 'top_hotsite'
            this.container = hao360.g(this.id);
            this.closeBtn = hao360.g('top-hotsite__btn--close');
            if (this.needHide()) return this.close();
            if (this.closeBtn) this.listenCloseBehavior();
        };

        proto.needHide = function () {
            var ua = navigator.userAgent;
            var match = ua.match(/MSIE (\d*.\d*)/);
            return (match && match.length && parseFloat(match[1]) < 7) || !this.expired();
        };

        proto.listenCloseBehavior = function () {
            var self = this;
            this.closeBtn.onclick = function () {
                self.close();
                self.setClosedCookie()
            };
        };

        proto.close = function () {
            this.container.parentNode.removeChild(this.container);
        };

        proto.setClosedCookie = function () {
            var cookieName = this.cookieName;
            var oneDay = 1000 * 3600 * 24;
            LogHub.behavior(this.id, 'close');
            qboot.cookie.set(cookieName, 1, {expires: oneDay});
        };

        proto.expired = function () {
            var cookieName = this.cookieName;
            return !qboot.cookie.get(cookieName);
        };

        new TopHotsite();
    })();
</script>

<script>
    window.Individual && Individual.hotsite();
    (function () {
        /**
         * 绑定事件，兼容IE
         * @param obj
         * @param evt
         * @param fn
         */
        var addEvent = function (obj, evt, fn) {
            obj && (typeof window.addEventListener === 'function') ? obj.addEventListener(evt, fn, false) : obj.attachEvent('on' + evt, fn);
        };

        /**
         * 请求域名 http/https
         */
        var domainGetter = (function () {
            var maps = {
                'interest-baidu': {
                    http: 'http://behavior.dhrest.com/hao360cn/hotsite1',
                    https: 'https://behavior.ssl.dhrest.com/hao360cn/hotsite1'
                },
                'interest-fenghuang': {
                    http: 'http://behavior.dhrest.com/hao360cn/hotsite2',
                    https: 'https://behavior.ssl.dhrest.com/hao360cn/hotsite2'
                },
                recommend: {
                    http: 'http://show.g.mediav.com/s',
                    https: 'https://show-g.mediav.com/s'
                }
            };

            var protocol = hao360.isHttps() ? 'https' : 'http';

            return function (key) {
                return maps[key] ? maps[key][protocol] : '';
            }
        })();

        /**
         * 打点统计模块, 因为广告数据由一条变成两条，所以实现方式需要改成面向对象的方式
         * @type {{pv, click}} 
         */
        function Adtracker(options){
            this.defaultOptions = options;
        }
        Adtracker.prototype.pv = function() {
            var imptk = this.defaultOptions.imptk,
                imparg = this.defaultOptions.imparg,
                impurl = this.defaultOptions.impurl;
            while (imptk && imptk.length) {
                logPureSender(imptk.shift());
            }
            if (impurl + imparg) {
                logPureSender(impurl + imparg);
            }
        }
        Adtracker.prototype.click = function (clktk) {
            if (clktk && clktk.length) {
                clktk.forEach(function (item) {
                    logPureSender(item);
                });
            }
        }

        /**
         * 兴趣记录缓存-localstorage
         * @type {{get, set}}
         */
        var interestStore = (function () {
            var appData = new AppData('api.hao.360.cn'),
                prefix = 'famoussite-interest-',
                expire = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;

            return {
                get: function (key) {
                    return appData.get(prefix + key);
                },
                set: function (key, value) {
                    appData.set(prefix + key, value, +(new Date) + expire);
                }
            }
        })();


        /**
         * 兴趣记录缓存-cookie
         * @type {{set, get}}
         */
        var interestRecord = (function () {
            var prefix = 'famoussite-';
            return {
                set: function (key, value) {
                    qboot.cookie.set(prefix + key, value || 1, {
                        expires: 30 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000
                    });
                },
                get: function (key) {
                    return qboot.cookie.get(prefix + key);
                }
            }
        })();

        /**
         * 名站网址推荐模块
         * @type {{init}}
         */
        var fsModule = (function () {

            /**
             * 监听事件
             */
            var bindEvent = function () {
                /**
                 * 对风景、军事点击行为进行统计，写入cookie
                 */
                addEvent(hao360.g('famoussite-fenghuang'), 'click', function (event) {
                    interestRecord.set('fenghuang', 1);
                });
                addEvent(hao360.g('famoussite-junshi'), 'click', function (event) {
                    interestRecord.set('fenghuang', 1);
                });
            };

            /**
             * 请求兴趣接口
             * @param cate
             * @param callback
             */
            var behavior = function (cate, callback) {
                qboot.jsonp(domainGetter(cate), {
                    fmt: 'jsonp',
                    huid: hao360.queryUrl(location.href, 'huid') || qboot.cookie.get('__huid')
                }, function (res) {
                    if (res && res.errno == 0) {
                        callback && callback(res.data);
                    }
                }, {
                    jsonp: '_callback'
                });
            };

            /**
             * 对PMP广告接口数据进行格式化
             * @param key
             * @param data
             * @returns {*}
             */
            var format = function (key, data) {
                try {
                    var ret;
                    var rlt = [];
                    for (var i = 0; i < data['adspaces'][key]['ads'].length; i++) {
                        ret = data['adspaces'][key]['ads'][i];
                        rlt.push({
                            impurl: data['impurl'],
                            imparg: ret.imparg,
                            imptk: ret.imptk,
                            clktk: ret.clktk.join('|'),
                            text: ret.desc,
                            url: ret.curl
                        });
                    }
                    return rlt;
                }
                catch (e) {
                    return [];
                }
            };

            /**
             * 加载PMP广告数据
             * @param callback
             */
            var loadPMPData = function (callback) {
                var showids = '1QrGjU';
                qboot.jsonp(domainGetter('recommend'), {
                    type: 1,
                    of: 4,
                    newf: 2,
                    showids: showids
                }, function (res) {
                    var recData = format(showids, res);
                    if (recData) {
                        callback && callback(recData);
                    }
                }, {
                    jsonp: 'jsonp'
                });
            };

            
            /**
             * 获取以广告左上角为原点的点击位置
             */
             var getXYAxis = function(e, item) {
                var axisDom = W(item).getXY() || [];
                var xDom = axisDom[0];
                var yDom = axisDom[1]; 
                return [parseInt(e.pageX-xDom), parseInt(e.pageY-yDom)];
            }

            /*
            * 宏替换,刷新时间戳防作弊
            * @params event 点击事件，用于获取点击坐标
            * @params item 需进行替换curl和clktk的dom
            * @params data 对应的原始单个广告数据
            * @params type 指明是鼠标开始点击还是结束点击
            */
            var updateStamp = function(event, item, data, type) {
                if (!data.clktk || !data.url) {
                    return
                }

                var clktk, url;
                var $aItem = W(item).attr('href') ? W(item) : W(item).query('a'); 
                var timeStamp = new Date().getTime();
                var xyAxis = getXYAxis(event, item);
                var xAxis = xyAxis[0];
                var yAxis = xyAxis[1];

                // 鼠标按下时将对应的宏替换
                if (type === 'start') {
                    clktk = data.clktk.replace(/__EVENT_TIME_START__/g, timeStamp)
                                 .replace(/__OFFSET_X__/g, xAxis)
                                 .replace(/__OFFSET_Y__/g, yAxis);
                    url = data.url.replace(/__EVENT_TIME_START__/g, timeStamp)
                                  .replace(/__OFFSET_X__/g, xAxis)
                                  .replace(/__OFFSET_Y__/g, yAxis);
                } else if (type === 'end') {
                    // 鼠标抬起时将对应的宏替换
                    clktk = W(item).attr('data-clktk').replace(/__EVENT_TIME_END__/g, timeStamp);
                    url = $aItem.attr('href').replace(/__EVENT_TIME_END__/g, timeStamp);
                } else {
                    clktk = data.clktk;
                    url = data.url;
                }

                $aItem.attr('data-clktk', clktk);
                $aItem.attr('href', url);
            }

            /**
             * 渲染广告并监听事件
             * @param data
             */
            var render = function (id, data, adtracker) {
                var element = hao360.g(id);
                if(!element){return;}
                var container = element.parentNode;
                
                // 更新 DOM
                container.innerHTML = R.tmpl('<a href="{url}" data-clktk="{clktk}">{text}</a>', data);
                var children = container.children[0];
                var clktk;
                addEvent(children, 'click', function () {
                    // 执行广告点击打点
                    clktk = W(this).attr('data-clktk').split('|');     
                    adtracker.click(clktk);

                    LogHub.behavior('famoussite-pmp', 'click');
                });
               
                addEvent(children, 'mousedown', function (e) {
                    // 鼠标按下时更新 url 和 clktk
		            updateStamp(e, W(this), data, 'start');
                });
                
                addEvent(children, 'mouseup', function (e) {
                    // 鼠标抬起时更新 url 和 clktk
	                updateStamp(e, W(this), data, 'end');
                });

                // 初始化并执行广告打点
                adtracker.pv();
            };

            /**
             * 更新本地缓存中的兴趣数据
             * @param callback
             */
            var update = function (callback) {
                /**
                 * 请求"凤凰、军事"位置的兴趣接口
                 */
                behavior('interest-fenghuang', function (data) {
                    // 将请求获得的结果写入本地缓存中
                    interestStore.set('fenghuang', data);
                    // 执行callback，参数需要进行转换，将数字转换为布尔值
                    callback && callback(!!parseInt(data));
                });
            };

            /**
             * 校验当前用户的兴趣，如当前兴趣缺失，则请求server接口
             * @param callback
             */
            var verify = function (callback) {
                var localCtk = interestRecord.get('fenghuang') == 1,   //cookie记录中，有过点击行为
                    remoteCtk = interestStore.get('fenghuang') == 0,   //远程日志记录中，有过点击行为
                    remoteUnctk = interestStore.get('fenghuang') == 1, //远程日志记录中，无点击行为
                    brokenToken = !qboot.cookie.get('__guid'),         //cookie被清理
                    previewMode = hao360.queryUrl(location.href, 'from') == 'pmp', //预览模式
                    hasUpdated = false;
                /**
                 * 如果该用户有清理过cookie或该用户点击过"凤凰、军事"，则不执行推荐
                 */
                if (brokenToken || localCtk || remoteCtk) {
                    callback(false);
                }
                /**
                 * 如果该用户未点击过"凤凰、军事"或现在属于预览模式，则执行推荐
                 */
                else if (remoteUnctk || previewMode) {
                    callback(true);
                }
                /**
                 *  更新缓存
                 */
                else {
                    update(function (ret) {
                        callback(ret);
                    });
                    hasUpdated = true;
                }
                /**
                 *  判断是否已经更新过缓存，如否，则更新缓存
                 */
                if (!hasUpdated) {
                    update();
                }
            };

            return {
                init: function () {
                    // 执行PMP推荐策略
                    loadPMPData(function (data) {
                        // pmp推荐策略现在有两个位置分别为 12306 和 kuaizixun
                        var famoussiteId = ['famoussite-12306', 'famoussite-kuaizixun'];
                        var adtracker;
                        for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
                            if (famoussiteId[i]) {
                                /**
                                 * 渲染广告数据
                                 */
                                adtracker = new Adtracker(data[i]);
                                render(famoussiteId[i], data[i], adtracker);
                                /**
                                 * 执行自定义行为打点
                                 */
                                LogHub.behavior('famoussite-pmp', 'pv');
                            }
                        }                                
                    });

                    // 凤凰军事暂时下线
                    // bindEvent();
                    /**
                     * 校验用户兴趣，判断该用户是否有过"凤凰、军事"的点击行为
                     */
                    // verify(function (valid) {
                    //     /**
                    //      * 如果该用户未点击过"凤凰、军事"，则认为该用户对"凤凰、军事"无兴趣，执行PMP推荐策略
                    //      */
                    //     if (valid) {
                    //         /**
                    //          * 加载广告数据
                    //          */
                    //         loadPMPData(function (data) {
                    //             /**
                    //              * 渲染数据
                    //              */
                    //             render('famoussite-fenghuang', data);
                    //             /***
                    //              * 初始化并执行广告打点
                    //              */
                    //             adtracker.init(data);
                    //             adtracker.pv();
                    //             /**
                    //              * 执行自定义行为打点
                    //              */
                    //             LogHub.behavior('famoussite-pmp', 'pv');
                    //         });
                    //     }
                    // });
                }
            }
        })();

        fsModule.init();
    })();
</script>		<div class="front-view-lb" id="hotsite-view-front"></div>

<script>
    (function () {
        function TopHotsiteBottom () {
            this.init();
        }
        var proto = TopHotsiteBottom.prototype;

        proto.init = function () {
            this.cookieName = 'top-hotsite-bottom-close';
            this.id = 'bottom_hotsite'
            this.container = hao360.g(this.id);
            this.closeBtn = hao360.g('bottom-hotsite__btn--close');
            if (this.needHide()) return this.close();
            if (this.closeBtn) this.listenCloseBehavior();
        };

        proto.needHide = function () {
            var ua = navigator.userAgent;
            var match = ua.match(/MSIE (\d*.\d*)/);
            return (match && match.length && parseFloat(match[1]) < 7) || !this.expired();
        };

        proto.listenCloseBehavior = function () {
            var self = this;
            this.closeBtn.onclick = function () {
                self.close();
                self.setClosedCookie()
            };
        };

        proto.close = function () {
            this.container.parentNode.removeChild(this.container);
        };

        proto.setClosedCookie = function () {
            var cookieName = this.cookieName;
            var oneDay = 1000 * 3600 * 24;
            LogHub.behavior(this.id, 'close');
            qboot.cookie.set(cookieName, 1, {expires: oneDay});
        };

        proto.expired = function () {
            var cookieName = this.cookieName;
            return !qboot.cookie.get(cookieName);
        };

        new TopHotsiteBottom();
    })();
</script>

    (function () {
        /*
         * 配合 Storm 打点
         * baipan @ 2014-12-8
         */
        function report(project, data) {
            var HAO_MONITOR_HOST = STATIC_CONFIG.monitor.haoMonitor;
            var mix = qboot.mix,
                encodeURIJson = qboot.encodeURIJson;
            var monitorMap = {
                'hao360': 1,
                'hao360i': 8
            };

            if (monitorMap[project]) {
                var logData = mix({
                    cc: ObjectH.values(hao360.area.get()).join(),
                    appid: monitorMap[project]
                }, data, true);

                var url = HAO_MONITOR_HOST + 'stat.gif';

                var logUrl = url + '?' + encodeURIJson(logData);
                logSender(logUrl);
            }
        }

        function routine() {
            var PAGE_LOADED_TIME = (new Date).getTime();
            report('hao360i', {
                ht: HEAD_END_TIME - PAGE_START_TIME,
                rt: PAGE_READY_TIME - PAGE_START_TIME,
                lt: UNFOLD_TIME - PAGE_START_TIME,
                et: PAGE_LOADED_TIME - PAGE_START_TIME,
                sc: [window.screen.width, window.screen.height].join('x')
            });
        }

        if (SendTimeMoniter) {
            routine();
        }

    })();
    
    (function(){
        var clientWidth = window.screen.width;
        if(!clientWidth){
            return;
        }
        var arrScreen = [1920,1600,1440,1371,1366,1360,1300,1280,1200,1025,1024];
        for(var i = 0,len = arrScreen.length; i < len;i++){
            if(clientWidth >= arrScreen[i]){
                reportClientWidth = arrScreen[i];
                break;
            }else{
                reportClientWidth = 800;
            }
        }
        
        LogHub.behavior('screen', reportClientWidth);

        var clientWidth = window.screen.width;
        var docWidth = document.documentElement.clientWidth;
        if(clientWidth - docWidth > 100){
            LogHub.behavior('screen', 'different');
        }
        var changeScreen = false;
        W(document).receive("page-size-changed",function(e){
            var docWidth2 = document.documentElement.clientWidth;
            if(docWidth2 != docWidth && !changeScreen){
                LogHub.behavior('screen', 'change');
                changeScreen = true;
                setTimeout(function(){
                    LogHub.behavior('screen', docWidth2 - docWidth);

                }, 100)
            }
        });
    })();

<script type="text/javascript">(function(){try{var browserSkinUrl='chrome://theme/IDR_THEME_NTP_BLURED_BACKGROUND';var browserSkinClass='js-browser-skin';var browserSkinBlackClass='js-skin-black';var browserSkinWhiteClass='js-skin-white';var nativeApi={sid:function(){var sid=external.GetSID(window);return sid;}(),getWallpaperInfo:function(callback){external.AppCmd(this.sid,"","getWallpaperInfo","","",function(code,data){if(code!==0){return;}var ret=JSON.parse('['+data+']');callback&&callback(ret);});}};function checkPageTheme(){var customData=new AppData('api.hao.360.cn').get('newUserTheme');if((customData&&customData[0]!=='default')||(W('.theme_link').length>0&&W('#themeLink').css('display')!=='none')){return true;}else if(W('#background .bg-inner').css('background-image')!='none'){return true;}else{return false;}}function onSkinChange(){if(checkPageTheme()===true){return;}setPageWallpaper();}function onWallpaperInfoChange(){if(checkPageTheme()===true){return;}nativeApi.getWallpaperInfo(function(info){if(info&&(info[0]===false||info.length!==5)){removeSkin();return;}renderSkin(info);});}function setPageWallpaper(){nativeApi.getWallpaperInfo(function(info){if(info&&(info[0]===false||info.length!==5)){removeSkin();return;}var url=browserSkinUrl+'?t='+Math.floor(new Date().getTime()/1000);getAverageColor(url,function(imageData){W('#browser-skin').css({'background':'rgba('+imageData.join(',')+')'});renderSkin(info,url);W('body').addClass(browserSkinClass);var bgBlackOrWhite=RGB2BlackOrWhite.apply(null,imageData);if(bgBlackOrWhite==='white'){W('body').removeClass(browserSkinBlackClass).addClass(browserSkinWhiteClass);}else{W('body').removeClass(browserSkinWhiteClass).addClass(browserSkinBlackClass);}});});}function renderSkin(info,url){var classOption={'transform':'translate('+-info[1]+'px, '+-info[2]+'px)','width':info[3]+'px','height':info[4]+'px'};if(url!==undefined){classOption['background-image']='url('+url+')';}W('#browser-skin-inner').css(classOption);}function getAverageColor(url,callback){var canvas=document.createElement('canvas');var context=canvas.getContext('2d');var image=new Image();image.crossOrigin='Anonymous';image.onload=function(){context.drawImage(image,0,0,3,2);var imageData=context.getImageData(2,0,1,1).data;callback(imageData);};image.onerror=function(){removeSkin();};image.src=url;}function RGB2Gray(R,G,B){var gray=(R*299+G*587+B*114)/1000;return gray;}function RGB2BlackOrWhite(R,G,B){var gray=RGB2Gray(R,G,B);var color;if(gray<160){color="black";}else{color="white";}return color;}function removeSkin(){W('#browser-skin').css({'background':'none'});W('body').removeClass(browserSkinClass).removeClass(browserSkinBlackClass).removeClass(browserSkinWhiteClass);}function main(){window.onSkinChange=onSkinChange;window.onWallpaperInfoChange=onWallpaperInfoChange;window.themeView.action.on('theme:change',removeSkin);window.themeView.action.on('theme:restore',removeSkin);qboot.events.on('browserskin:render',onSkinChange);if(checkPageTheme()!==true){setPageWallpaper();}}main();}catch(e){}})();</script>
